,a.amount AS a_amount,a.amount_based AS a_amount_based,b.amount AS b_amount,b.amount_based AS b_amount_based,c.amount AS c_amount,c.amount_based AS c_amount_based 
  FROM erp_accounting_drdc.SelectAllChart chart LEFT JOIN(
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,0 AS chart_class_id,'CASH' AS chart_class_code,'CASH' AS chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.credit - a.debit AS amount,a.credit_based - a.debit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) = 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
	                  AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-01-31','%m-%Y') 
                    GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a
                UNION
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,a.chart_class_id,a.chart_class_code,a.chart_class_name,a.validation

  FROM erp_accounting_drdc.SelectAllChart chart LEFT JOIN(
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,0 AS chart_class_id,'CASH' AS chart_class_code,'CASH' AS chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.credit - a.debit AS amount,a.credit_based - a.debit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name

	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) = 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
	                  AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-04-30','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'

,a.amount AS a_amount,a.amount_based AS a_amount_based 
  FROM erp_accounting_drdc.SelectAllChart chart LEFT JOIN(
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,0 AS chart_class_id,'CASH' AS chart_class_code,'CASH' AS chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.credit - a.debit AS amount,a.credit_based - a.debit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) = 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
	                  AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-04-30','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'
                    GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a
                UNION
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,a.chart_class_id,a.chart_class_code,a.chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.debit - a.credit AS amount,a.debit_based - a.credit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) <> 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''

,a.amount AS a_amount,a.amount_based AS a_amount_based,b.amount AS b_amount,b.amount_based AS b_amount_based,c.amount AS c_amount,c.amount_based AS c_amount_based 
  FROM erp_accounting_drdc.SelectAllChart chart LEFT JOIN(
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,0 AS chart_class_id,'CASH' AS chart_class_code,'CASH' AS chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.credit - a.debit AS amount,a.credit_based - a.debit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) = 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
	                  AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-04-30','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'
                    GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a
                UNION
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,a.chart_class_id,a.chart_class_code,a.chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.debit - a.credit AS amount,a.debit_based - a.credit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) <> 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
                      AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-04-30','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'
	                GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a ) a ON a.account_id = chart.account_id LEFT JOIN(
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,0 AS chart_class_id,'CASH' AS chart_class_code,'CASH' AS chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.credit - a.debit AS amount,a.credit_based - a.debit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id

	                  AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-05-31','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'

                ) a

	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) <> 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
                      AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-05-31','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'
	                GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a ) b ON b.account_id = chart.account_id LEFT JOIN(
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,0 AS chart_class_id,'CASH' AS chart_class_code,'CASH' AS chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.credit - a.debit AS amount,a.credit_based - a.debit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) = 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
	                  AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-06-30','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'
                    GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a
                UNION
                SELECT a.account_id,a.account_code,a.account_name,a.chart_class_id,a.chart_class_code,a.chart_class_name,a.validation
                ,a.debit - a.credit AS amount,a.debit_based - a.credit_based AS amount_based
                FROM (
	                SELECT a.trans_id,a.trans_no,a.trans_date
	                ,a.book_id,d.book_code,d.book_name
	                ,a.journal_id,f.journal_code,f.journal_name
	                ,b.jbooks_id,b.account_id,c.account_code,c.account_name,c.validation
	                ,c.chart_class_id,e.chart_class_code,e.chart_class_name
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit,0)) AS debit,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit,0)) AS credit
	                ,SUM(IFNULL(b.debit_based,0)) AS debit_based,SUM(IFNULL(b.credit_based,0)) AS credit_based
	                FROM trans_header a
	                LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_chart c ON c.account_id = b.account_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_book d ON d.book_id = a.book_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_acc_chart_class e ON e.chart_class_id = c.chart_class_id
	                LEFT JOIN erp_fs_drdc.lib_erp_journal f ON f.journal_id = a.journal_id
	                WHERE a.journal_id = 4 AND IFNULL(c.validation,0) <> 1 AND UPPER(IFNULL(a.status,'')) <> 'C' AND IFNULL(b.jbooks_id,'') <> ''
                      AND DATE_FORMAT(a.trans_date,'%m-%Y') = DATE_FORMAT('2019-06-30','%m-%Y')  AND a.book_id = '13'
	                GROUP BY c.account_id
	                ORDER BY c.validation
                ) a ) c ON c.account_id = chart.account_id 
                    WHERE (a.amount <> 0 AND a.amount_based <> 0) OR (b.amount <> 0 AND b.amount_based <> 0) OR (c.amount <> 0 AND c.amount_based <> 0) ORDER BY chart_class_id
